[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`udev_rule_parse_value` function within systemd's udev-rules.c file. The [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer identified a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation that attempts to write beyond [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe allocated heap buffer boundary, occurring at line [0m[1;36m1223[0m[39m of the udev-rules.c [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msource file. This issue was discovered through fuzzing the [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fuzz-udev-rule-parse-value` target.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability, specifically a write operation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat exceeds allocated memory boundaries. The SCARINESS score is [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m, indicating a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-write-heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests when the fuzzer executes the `udev_rule_parse_value` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction with specially crafted input. According to the AddressSanitizer report:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Location**: The overflow occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x5020000000d7[0m[39m`, which is precisely[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocated region spanning from `[0m[1;36m0x5020000000d0[0m[39m` to [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x5020000000d7[0m[39m`[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Operation Type**: A WRITE of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at the boundary of the allocated buffer[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Trigger Point**: Line [0m[1;36m1223[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m in [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/work/build/../../src/systemd/src/udev/[0m[95mudev-rules.c[0m[39m`[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue originates from the following execution path:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `fuzz-udev-rule-parse-value.c` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m22[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allocates memory and calls the target function[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The memory allocation occurs at line [0m[1;36m18[0m[39m of the fuzzer harness using malloc[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The actual overflow happens in `udev_rule_parse_value` when processing the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer-provided input[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Allocation Context[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe problematic memory region is a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte heap allocation made by the fuzzer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness. The shadow memory dump shows:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The allocated region is marked with `[0m[1;36m07[0m[39m` in the shadow bytes, indicating [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccessible bytes[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Surrounding regions are marked with `fa` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mheap redzones[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which are protective [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mzones[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The write operation attempts to access the byte immediately after this [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Important Observations[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The vulnerability is reproducible with a specific testcase file [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The fuzzer configuration includes:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - RSS limit: [0m[1;36m2560[0m[39m MB[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Timeout: [0m[1;36m25[0m[39m seconds[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Running mode: interactive[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzzing engine: libfuzzer[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The overflow occurs during value parsing operations in the udev rules processing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The vulnerability involves string or buffer manipulation where bounds checking [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappears insufficient[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following areas [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be investigated:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Location**: `src/udev/udev-rules.c` at line [0m[1;36m1223[0m[39m - examine the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecific write operation and the logic determining buffer boundaries[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Function Context**: The complete `udev_rule_parse_value` function [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation to understand:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Input validation mechanisms[0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39munderstand:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Related Functions**: Any helper functions called by `udev_rule_parse_value` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat handle buffer operations or string processing[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1212[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35massert[0m[1;39m([0m[39ml <= i - [0m[1;39m([0m[39mm + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1217[0m[39m:                *[0m[35m/[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1218[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mis_prefix_match[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1219[0m[39m:                        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* need more room to make rule glob match *[0m[35m/[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1220[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr + pos - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, unescaped, l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1221[0m[39m:                        str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'*'[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1222[0m[39m:                        str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1223[0m[39m:                        str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1224[0m[39m:                        m = str + pos - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1225[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1226[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1227[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mm, unescaped, l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1228[0m[39m:                        m[0m[1;39m[[0m[39ml[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1229[0m[39m:                        m[0m[1;39m[[0m[39ml + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1230[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1231[0m[39m:                str = m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1232[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1233[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1234[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1235[0m[39m:        *ret_value = str;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1236[0m[39m:        *ret_endpos = i + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1237[0m[39m:        *ret_is_case_insensitive = is_case_insensitive;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1238[0m[39m:        return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1239[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for Heap-Buffer-Overflow in `udev_rule_parse_value`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs in `src/udev/udev-rules.c` at line [0m[1;36m1223[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand similarly at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m1229[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the `udev_rule_parse_value` function. The function writes beyond [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated buffer boundaries when processing escaped strings. Specifically:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m1223[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mescaped + prefix match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m1229[0m[39m** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mescaped, no prefix match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: `m[0m[1;39m[[0m[39ml + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m` where `m = str + pos`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBoth paths write to position `pos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` without validating this position is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the allocated buffer. The function assumes sufficient buffer space exists [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor the unescaped content plus terminating characters [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m extra bytes: [0m[32m'*'[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'\0'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'\0'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer allocates exactly `size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes with no trailing space[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Production code uses `[0m[1;35mstrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which allocates exactly `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. When a value appears at the end of a line with specific `pos` and `l` [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcombinations, the calculated write position exceeds buffer bounds[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Why Current Code Works in Production [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUsually[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe production code path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`rule_add_line` → `parse_line` → `udev_rule_parse_value`[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypically works because:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines contain multiple [0m[33mkey[0m[39m=[0m[35mvalue[0m[39m pairs with trailing content[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A value in the middle of a line has unused buffer space after it[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function reuses prefix character space and writes into trailing space[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only values at line end with minimal trailing content would expose the overflow[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Implementation Strategy[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe optimal fix is to **validate the required buffer space before performing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrites** in the escaped path. This preserves the in-place modification strategy [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile preventing overflows.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Calculate Required Buffer Space[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBefore performing any writes in the escaped path [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m1212[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, calculate the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximum write position:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For prefix match: maximum write is at `pos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor the second null [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminator[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For non-prefix match: maximum write is at `pos + l + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msame, via `m[0m[1;39m[[0m[39ml + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe minimum write position is `pos - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor prefix match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or `pos` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor non-prefix[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Determine Available Buffer Space[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe original string position where parsing started is `str`. The ending position of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe quoted value is at `i` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe closing quote[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. We need to ensure that writes don't[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgo beyond `i + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich points just after the closing quote, where subsequent [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent might exist[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe key insight: the function should only write within the span from the prefix [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart to just past the closing quote. Calculate:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize_t available_space = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - str;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m From start to past closing quote[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Validate Before Writing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEscaped + Prefix Match Path[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Alternative Approach: Ensure Sufficient Allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCaller Side[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf modifying `udev_rule_parse_value` is insufficient, consider ensuring callers [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### In `rule_add_line` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m1339[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize_t len = [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mline_str[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!line[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return [0m[1;35mlog_oom[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mstrcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mline, line_str[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, this approach is **NOT RECOMMENDED** because:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It wastes memory for all lines [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmost don't need extra space[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It doesn't fix the fuzzer harness issue[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function should be self-defensive[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Recommended Approach Summary[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix: Add bounds validation in `udev_rule_parse_value`**[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. After line [0m[1;36m1212[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mescaped path[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, before the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mis_prefix_match[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Calculate available space: `size_t available = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - str`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. In the prefix match branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore line [0m[1;36m1220[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Validate: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m > available[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return -ENOBUFS;`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. In the non-prefix match branch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore line [0m[1;36m1227[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Validate: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpos + l + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m > available[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return -ENOBUFS;`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. In the non-escaped path, after the loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore line [0m[1;36m1187[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-ENOBUFS;`[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis approach:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Fixes the vulnerability without changing the API[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Preserves in-place modification for efficiency[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Returns error for malformed/truncated input [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcorrect behavior[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Doesn't break existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwell-formed inputs pass validation[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Protects against future fuzzer-discovered edge cases[0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Error Code Choice[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUse `-ENOBUFS` or `-EINVAL`:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `-ENOBUFS`: [0m[32m"No buffer space available"[0m[39m - semantically accurate for insufficient [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspace[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `-EINVAL`: [0m[32m"Invalid argument"[0m[39m - consistent with other validation errors in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRecommendation: Use `-EINVAL` for consistency with existing error returns in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1165[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1169[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1178[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1204[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Preserving Existing Logic[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix preserves all existing functionality:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
